   [ācārādhyāya]	[AcAra-aDyAya]
   [1. upodghātaprakaraṇam]	[1. upodGAta-prakaraNam]
   yogīśvaraṃ yājñavalkyaṃ saṃpūjya munayo 'bruvan /	yogi-ISvaram yAjQavalkyam saMpUjya munayaH abruvan /
   varṇāśrametarāṇāṃ no brūhi dharmān aśeṣataḥ // Yj_1.1 //	varNa-ASrama-itarANAm naH brUhi DarmAn aSezatas // Yt-_1.1 //
   mithilāsthaḥ sa yogīndraḥ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvābravīn munīn /	miTilA-sTaH sa yogi-indraH kzaNam DyAtvA-abravIt munIn /
   yasmin deśe mṛgaḥ kṛṣṇas tasmin dharmān nibodhata // Yj_1.2 //	yasmin deSe mRgaH kRzNaH tasmin DarmAn niboData // Yt-_1.2 //
   purāṇanyāyamīmāṃsā- dharmaśāstrāṅgamiśritāḥ /	purANa-nyAya-mImAMsA Darma-SAstra-aFga-miSritAH /
   vedāḥ sthānāni vidyānāṃ dharmasya ca caturdaśa // Yj_1.3 //	vedAH sTAnAni vidyAnAm Darmasya ca caturdaSa // Yt-_1.3 //
   manvatriviṣṇuhārīta- yājñavalkyośano 'ṅgirāḥ /	manu-atri-vizNu-hArIta yAjQavalkya-uSanaH aFgirAH /
   yamāpastambasaṃvartāḥ kātyāyanabṛhaspatī // Yj_1.4 //	yama-apastamba-saMvartAH kAtyAyana-bRhaspatI // Yt-_1.4 //
   parāśaravyāsaśaṅkha- likhitā dakṣagautamau /	parASara-vyAsa-SaFKa liKitAH dakza-gOtamO /
   śātātapo vasiṣṭhaś ca dharmaśāstraprayojakāḥ // Yj_1.5 //	SAtAtapaH vasizWaH ca Darma-SAstra-prayojakAH // Yt-_1.5 //
   deśe kāla upāyena dravyaṃ śraddhāsamanvitam /	deSe kAle upAyena dravyam SradDA-samanvitam /
   pātre pradīyate yat tat sakalaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam // Yj_1.6 //	pAtre pradIyate yat tat sakalam Darma-lakzaNam // Yt-_1.6 //
   śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ sadācāraḥ svasya ca priyam ātmanaḥ /	SrutiH smRtiH sat-AcAraH svasya ca priyam AtmanaH /
   samyaksaṃkalpajaḥ kāmo dharmamūlam idaṃ smṛtam // Yj_1.7 //	samyak-saMkalpa-jaH kAmaH Darma-mUlam idam smRtam // Yt-_1.7 //
   ijyācāradamāhiṃsā- dānasvādhyāyakarmaṇām /	ijyA-cAra-dama-ahiMsA dAna-svADyAya-karmaNAm /
   ayaṃ tu paramo dharmo yad yogenātmadarśanam // Yj_1.8 //	ayam tu paramaH DarmaH yat yogena-Atma-darSanam // Yt-_1.8 //
   catvāro vedadharmajñāḥ parṣat traividyam eva vā /	catvAraH veda-Darma-jQAH parzad trEvidyam eva vA /
   sā brūte yaṃ sa dharmaḥ syād eko vādhyātmavittamaḥ // Yj_1.9 //	sA brUte yam sa DarmaH syAt ekaH vA-aDyAtma-vittamaH // Yt-_1.9 //
   [2. brahmacāriprakaraṇam]	[2. brahmacAri-prakaraNam]
   brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdrā varṇās tv ādyās trayo dvijāḥ /	brahma-kzatriya-viS-SUdrAH varNAH tu AdyAH trayaH dvijAH /
   niṣekādyāḥ śmaśānāntās teṣāṃ vai mantrataḥ kriyāḥ // Yj_1.10 //	nizeka-AdyAH SmaSAna-antAH tezAm vE mantrataH kriyAH // Yt-_1.10 //
   garbhādhānam ṛtau puṃsaḥ savanaṃ spandanāt purā /	garBADAnam RtO puMsaH savanam spandanAt purA /
   ṣaṣṭhe 'ṣṭame vā sīmanto māsy ete jātakarma ca // Yj_1.11 //	zazWe azwame vA sImantaH mAsi ete jAtakarma ca // Yt-_1.11 //
   ahany ekādaśe nāma caturthe māsi niṣkramaḥ /	ahani ekAdaSe nAma caturTe mAsi nizkramaH /
   ṣaṣṭhe 'nnaprāśanaṃ māsi cūḍā kāryā yathākulam // Yj_1.12 //	zazWe annaprASanam mAsi cUxA kAryA yaTA-kulam // Yt-_1.12 //
   evam enaḥ śamaṃ yāti bījagarbhasamudbhavam /	evam enaH Samam yAti bIja-garBa-samudBavam /
   tūṣṇīm etāḥ kriyāḥ strīṇāṃ vivāhas tu samantrakaḥ // Yj_1.13 //	tUzNIm etAH kriyAH strINAm vivAhaH tu sa-mantrakaH // Yt-_1.13 //
   garbhāṣṭame 'ṣṭame vābde brāhmaṇasyopanāyanam /	garBa-azwame azwame vA-abde brAhmaNasya-upanAyanam /
   rājñām ekādaśe saike viśām eke yathākulam // Yj_1.14 //	rAjQAm ekAdaSe sA-eke viSAm eke yaTA-kulam // Yt-_1.14 //
   upanīya guruḥ śiṣyaṃ mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakam /	upanIya guruH Sizyam mahAvyAhRti-pUrvakam /
   vedam adhyāpayed enaṃ śaucācārāṃś ca śikṣayet // Yj_1.15 //	vedam aDyApayet enam SOca-AcArAn ca Sikzayet // Yt-_1.15 //
   divāsaṃdhyāsu karṇastha- brahmasūtrodaṅmukhaḥ /	divA-saMDyAsu karNa-sTa brahmasUtra-udaFmuKaH /
   kuryān mūtrapurīṣe ca rātrau ced dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ // Yj_1.16 //	kuryAt mUtra-purIze ca rAtrO ced dakziNAmuKaH // Yt-_1.16 //
   gṛhītaśiśnaś cotthāya mṛdbhir abhyuddhṛtair jalaiḥ /	gRhIta-SiSnaH ca-utTAya mRdBiH aByudDRtEH jalEH /
   gandhalepakṣayakaraṃ śaucaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ // Yj_1.17 //	ganDa-lepa-kzaya-karam SOcam kuryAt atandritaH // Yt-_1.17 //
   antarjānu śucau deśa upaviṣṭa udaṅmukhaḥ /	antar-jAnu SucO deSaH upavizwaH udaFmuKaH /
   prāg vā brāhmeṇa tīrthena dvijo nityam upaspṛśet // Yj_1.18 //	prAk vA brAhmeNa tIrTena dvijaH nityam upaspRSet // Yt-_1.18 //
   kaniṣṭhādeśinyaṅguṣṭha- mūlāny agraṃ karasya ca /	kanizWA-deSinI-aFguzWa mUlAni agram karasya ca /
   prajāpatipitṛbrahma- devatīrthāny anukramāt // Yj_1.19 //	prajApati-pitR-brahma deva-tIrTAni anukramAt // Yt-_1.19 //
   triḥ prāśyāpo dvir unmṛjya khāny adbhiḥ samupaspṛśet /	tris prASya-apaH dvis unmRjya KAni adBiH samupaspRSet /
   adbhis tu prakṛtisthābhir hīnābhiḥ phenabudbudaiḥ // Yj_1.20 //	adBiH tu prakRti-sTABiH hInABiH Pena-budbudEH // Yt-_1.20 //
   hṛtkaṇṭhatālugābhis tu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ dvijātayaḥ /	hRd-kaNWa-tAlu-gABiH tu yaTAsaMKyam dvijAtayaH /
   śudhyeran strī ca śūdraś ca sakṛt spṛṣṭābhir antataḥ // Yj_1.21 //	SuDyeran strI ca SUdraH ca sakRt spRzwABiH antatas // Yt-_1.21 //
   snānam abdaivatair mantrair mārjanaṃ prāṇasaṃyamaḥ /	snAnam ap-dEvatEH mantrEH mArjanam prANa-saMyamaH /
   sūryasya cāpy upasthānaṃ gāyatryāḥ pratyahaṃ japaḥ // Yj_1.22 //	sUryasya ca-api upasTAnam gAyatryAH pratyaham japaH // Yt-_1.22 //
   gāyatrīṃ śirasā sārdhaṃ japed vyāhṛtipūrvikām /	gAyatrIm SirasA sArDam japet vyAhRti-pUrvikAm /
   pratipraṇavasaṃyuktāṃ trir ayaṃ prāṇasaṃyamaḥ // Yj_1.23 //	prati-praNava-saMyuktAm tris ayam prANa-saMyamaH // Yt-_1.23 //
   prāṇān āyamya saṃprokṣya tṛcenābdaivatena tu /	prANAn Ayamya saMprokzya tRcena-abdEvatena tu /
   japann āsīta sāvitrīṃ pratyag ātārakodayāt // Yj_1.24 //	japan AsIta sAvitrIm pratyak AtAraka-udayAt // Yt-_1.24 //
   saṃdhyāṃ prāk prātar evaṃ hi tiṣṭhed āsūryadarśanāt /	saMDyAm prAk prAtar evam hi tizWet AsUrya-darSanAt /
   agnikāryaṃ tataḥ kuryāt saṃdhyayor ubhayor api // Yj_1.25 //	agni-kAryam tatas kuryAt saMDyayoH uBayoH api // Yt-_1.25 //
   tato 'bhivādayed vṛddhān asāv aham iti bruvan /	tatas aBivAdayet vRdDAn asO aham iti bruvan /
   guruṃ caivāpy upāsīta svādhyāyārthaṃ samāhitaḥ // Yj_1.26 //	gurum ca-eva-api upAsIta svADyAya-arTam samAhitaH // Yt-_1.26 //
   āhūtaś cāpy adhīyīta labdhaṃ cāsmai nivedayet /	AhUtaH ca-api aDIyIta labDam ca-asmE nivedayet /
   hitaṃ tasyācaren nityaṃ manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ // Yj_1.27 //	hitam tasya-Acaret nityam manaH-vAc-kAya-karmaBiH // Yt-_1.27 //
   kṛtajñādrohimedhāvi- śucikalyānasūyakāḥ /	kRtajQA-drohi-meDAvi Suci-kalya-anasUyakAH /
   adhyāpyā dharmataḥ sādhu śaktāptajñānavittadāḥ // Yj_1.28 //	aDyApyAH DarmataH sADu Sakta-Apta-jQAna-vitta-dAH // Yt-_1.28 //
   daṇḍājinopavītāni mekhalāṃ caiva dhārayet /	daNxa-ajina-upavItAni meKalAm ca-eva DArayet /
   brāhmaṇeṣu cared bhaikṣam anindyeṣv ātmavṛttaye // Yj_1.29 //	brAhmaNezu caret BEkzam anindyezu Atma-vRttaye // Yt-_1.29 //
   ādimadhyāvasāneṣu bhavacchabdopalakṣitā /	Adi-maDya-avasAnezu Bavat-Sabda-upalakzitA /
   brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ bhaikṣacaryā yathākramam // Yj_1.30 //	brAhmaNa-kzatriya-viSAm BEkza-caryA yaTAkramam // Yt-_1.30 //
   kṛtāgnikāryo bhuñjīta vāgyato gurvanujñayā /	kRta-agni-kAryaH BuQjIta vAgyataH guru-anujQayA /
   āpośānakriyāpūrvaṃ satkṛtyānnam akutsayan // Yj_1.31 //	ApoSAna-kriyA-pUrvam satkRtya-annam akutsayan // Yt-_1.31 //
   brahmacarye sthito naikam annam adyād anāpadi /	brahmacarye sTitaH na-ekam annam adyAt anApadi /
   brāhmaṇaḥ kāmam aśnīyāc chrāddhe vratam apīḍayan // Yj_1.32 //	brAhmaNaH kAmam aSnIyAt SrAdDe vratam apIxayan // Yt-_1.32 //
   madhumāṃsāñjanocchiṣṭa- śuktastrīprāṇihiṃsanam /	maDu-mAMsa-aQjana-ucCizwa Sukta-strI-prANi-hiMsanam /
   bhāskarālokanāślīla- parivādādi varjayet // Yj_1.33 //	BAskara-Alokana-aSlIla parivAda-Adi varjayet // Yt-_1.33 //
   sa gurur yaḥ kriyāḥ kṛtvā vedam asmai prayacchati /	sa guruH yaH kriyAH kRtvA vedam asmE prayacCati /
   upanīya dadad vedam ācāryaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ // Yj_1.34 //	upanIya dadat vedam AcAryaH saH udAhRtaH // Yt-_1.34 //
   ekadeśam upādhyāya ṛtvig yajñakṛd ucyate /	eka-deSam upADyAyaH Rtvij yajQa-kRt ucyate /
   ete mānyā yathāpūrvam ebhyo mātā garīyasī // Yj_1.35 //	ete mAnyAH yaTApUrvam eByaH mAtA garIyasI // Yt-_1.35 //
   prativedaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dvādaśābdāni pañca vā /	prativedam brahmacaryam dvAdaSa-abdAni paQca vA /
   grahaṇāntikam ity eke keśāntaś caiva ṣoḍaśe // Yj_1.36 //	grahaNa-antikam iti eke keSAntaH ca-eva zoxaSe // Yt-_1.36 //
   āṣoḍaśād ādvāviṃśāc caturviṃśāc ca vatsarāt /	AzoxaSAt AdvAviMSAt caturviMSAt ca vatsarAt /
   brahmakṣatraviśāṃ kālaupanāyanikaḥ paraḥ // Yj_1.37 //	brahma-kzatra-viSAm kAla-OpanAyanikaH paraH // Yt-_1.37 //
   ata ūrdhvaṃ patanty ete sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ /	atas UrDvam patanti ete sarva-Darma-bahizkRtAH /
   sāvitrīpatitā vrātyā vrātyastomād ṛte kratoḥ // Yj_1.38 //	sAvitrIpatitAH vrAtyAH vrAtyastomAt Rte kratoH // Yt-_1.38 //
   mātur yad agre jāyante dvitīyaṃ mauñjibandhanāt /	mAtuH yat agre jAyante dvitIyam mOQjibanDanAt /
   brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśas tasmād ete dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ // Yj_1.39 //	brAhmaNa-kzatriya-viSaH tasmAt ete dvijAH smRtAH // Yt-_1.39 //
   yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva śubhānāṃ caiva karmaṇām /	yajQAnAm tapasAm ca-eva SuBAnAm ca-eva karmaNAm /
   veda eva dvijātīnāṃ niḥśreyasakaraḥ paraḥ // Yj_1.40 //	vedaH eva dvijAtInAm niHSreyasa-karaH paraH // Yt-_1.40 //
   madhunā payasā caiva sa devāṃs tarpayed dvijaḥ /	maDunA payasA ca-eva sa devAn tarpayet dvijaH /
   pitṝn madhughṛtābhyāṃ ca ṛco 'dhīte ca yo 'nvaham // Yj_1.41 //	pitLn maDu-GRtAByAm ca RcaH aDIte ca yaH anvaham // Yt-_1.41 //
   yajūṃṣi śaktito 'dhīte yo 'nvahaṃ sa ghṛtāmṛtaiḥ /	yajUMzi SaktitaH aDIte yaH anvaham sa GRta-amRtEH /
   prīṇāti devān ājyena madhunā ca pitṝṃs tathā // Yj_1.42 //	prINAti devAn Ajyena maDunA ca pitLn taTA // Yt-_1.42 //
   sa tu somaghṛtair devāṃs tarpayed yo 'nvahaṃ paṭhet /	sa tu soma-GRtEH devAn tarpayet yaH anvaham paWet /
   sāmāni tṛptiṃ kuryāc ca pitṝṇāṃ madhusarpiṣā // Yj_1.43 //	sAmAni tRptim kuryAt ca pitLNAm maDu-sarpizA // Yt-_1.43 //
   medasā tarpayed devān atharvāṅgirasaḥ paṭhan /	medasA tarpayet devAn aTarva-aFgirasaH paWan /
   pitṝṃś ca madhusarpirbhyām anvahaṃ śaktito dvijaḥ // Yj_1.44 //	pitLn ca maDu-sarpirByAm anvaham SaktitaH dvijaH // Yt-_1.44 //
   vākovākyaṃ purāṇaṃ ca nārāśaṃsīś ca gāthikāḥ /	vAkovAkyam purANam ca nArASaMsIH ca gATikAH /
   itihāsāṃs tathā vidyāḥ śaktyādhīte hi yo 'nvaham // Yj_1.45 //	itihAsAn taTA vidyAH SaktyA-aDIte hi yaH anvaham // Yt-_1.45 //
   māṃsakṣīraudanamadhu- tarpaṇaṃ sa divaukasām /	mAMsa-kzIra-odana-maDu tarpaNam sa divOkasAm /
   karoti tṛptiṃ kuryāc ca pitṝṇāṃ madhusarpiṣā // Yj_1.46 //	karoti tRptim kuryAt ca pitLNAm maDu-sarpizA // Yt-_1.46 //
   te tṛptās tarpayanty enaṃ sarvakāmaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ /	te tRptAH tarpayanti enam sarva-kAma-PalEH SuBEH /
   yaṃ yaṃ kratum adhīte ca tasya tasyāpnuyāt phalam // Yj_1.47 //	yam yam kratum aDIte ca tasya tasya-ApnuyAt Palam // Yt-_1.47 //
   trir vittapūrṇapṛthivī- dānasya phalam aśnute /	tris vitta-pUrNa-pRTivI dAnasya Palam aSnute /
   tapasaś ca parasyeha nityaṃ svādhyāyavān dvijaḥ // Yj_1.48 //	tapasaH ca parasya-iha nityam svADyAyavAn dvijaH // Yt-_1.48 //
   naiṣṭhiko brahmacārī tu vased ācāryasaṃnidhau /	nEzWikaH brahmacArI tu vaset AcArya-saMniDO /
   tadabhāve 'sya tanaye patnyāṃ vaiśvānare 'pi vā // Yj_1.49 //	tad-aBAve asya tanaye patnyAm vESvAnare api vA // Yt-_1.49 //
   anena vidhinā dehaṃ sādayan vijitendriyaḥ /	anena viDinA deham sAdayan vijita-indriyaH /
   brahmalokam avāpnoti na cehājāyate punaḥ // Yj_1.50 //	brahma-lokam avApnoti na ca-iha-AjAyate punar // Yt-_1.50 //
   [3. vivāhaprakaraṇam]	[3. vivAha-prakaraNam]
   gurave tu varaṃ dattvā snāyād vā tadanujñayā /	gurave tu varam dattvA snAyAt vA tad-anujQayA /
   vedaṃ vratāni vā pāraṃ nītvā hy ubhayam eva vā // Yj_1.51 //	vedam vratAni vA pAram nItvA hi uBayam eva vA // Yt-_1.51 //
   aviplutabrahmacaryo lakṣaṇyāṃ striyam udvahet /	avipluta-brahmacaryaH lakzaNyAm striyam udvahet /
   ananyapūrvikāṃ kāntām asapiṇḍāṃ yavīyasīm // Yj_1.52 //	ananya-pUrvikAm kAntAm asapiNxAm yavIyasIm // Yt-_1.52 //
   arogiṇīṃ bhrātṛmatīm asamānārṣagotrajān /	arogiNIm BrAtRmatIm asamAn-a-Arza-gotra-jAn /
   pañcamāt saptamād ūrdhvaṃ mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tathā // Yj_1.53 //	paQcamAt saptamAt UrDvam mAtRtaH pitRtaH taTA // Yt-_1.53 //
   daśapūruṣavikhyātāc chrotriyāṇāṃ mahākulāt /	daSa-pUruza-viKyAtAt SrotriyANAm mahA-kulAt /
   sphītād api na saṃcāri- rogadoṣasamanvitāt // Yj_1.54 //	sPItAt api na saMcAri roga-doza-samanvitAt // Yt-_1.54 //
   etair eva guṇair yuktaḥ savarṇaḥ śrotriyo varaḥ /	etEH eva guNEH yuktaH savarNaH SrotriyaH varaH /
   yatnāt parīkṣitaḥ puṃstve yuvā dhīmān janapriyaḥ // Yj_1.55 //	yatnAt parIkzitaH puMstve yuvA DImAn jana-priyaH // Yt-_1.55 //
   yad ucyate dvijātīnāṃ śūdrād dāropasaṃgrahaḥ /	yat ucyate dvijAtInAm SUdrAt dAra-upasaMgrahaH /
   naitan mama mataṃ yasmāt tatrāyaṃ jāyate svayam // Yj_1.56 //	na-etat mama matam yasmAt tatra-ayam jAyate svayam // Yt-_1.56 //
   tisro varṇānupūrvyeṇa dve tathaikā yathākramam /	tisraH varNa-AnupUrvyeNa dve taTA-ekA yaTAkramam /
   brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ bhāryā svā śūdrajanmanaḥ // Yj_1.57 //	brAhmaNa-kzatriya-viSAm BAryA svA SUdra-janmanaH // Yt-_1.57 //
   brāhmo vivāha āhūya dīyate śaktyalaṃkṛtā /	brAhmaH vivAhaH AhUya dIyate Sakti-alaMkRtA /
   tajjaḥ punāty ubhayataḥ puruṣān ekaviṃśatim // Yj_1.58 //	tad-jaH punAti uBayatas puruzAn ekaviMSatim // Yt-_1.58 //
   yajñastha ṛtvije daiva ādāyārṣas tu godvayam /	yajQa-sTaH Rtvije dEvaH AdAya-ArzaH tu go-dvayam /
   caturdaśa prathamajaḥ punāty uttarajaś ca ṣaṭ // Yj_1.59 //	caturdaSa praTama-jaH punAti uttara-jaH ca zaw // Yt-_1.59 //
   ity uktvā caratāṃ dharmaṃ saha yā dīyate 'rthine /	iti uktvA caratAm Darmam saha yA dIyate arTine /
   sa kāyaḥ pāvayet tajjaḥ ṣaṭ ṣaḍvaṃśyān sahātmanā // Yj_1.60 //	sa kAyaH pAvayet tad-jaH zaw zaz-vaMSyAn saha-AtmanA // Yt-_1.60 //
   āsuro draviṇādānād gāndharvaḥ samayān mithaḥ /	AsuraH draviNa-AdAnAt gAnDarvaH samayAt miTas /
   rākṣaso yuddhaharaṇāt paiśācaḥ kanyakāchalāt // Yj_1.61 //	rAkzasaH yudDa-haraNAt pESAcaH kanyakA-CalAt // Yt-_1.61 //
   pāṇir grāhyaḥ savarṇāsu gṛhṇīyāt kṣatriyā śaram /	pANiH grAhyaH savarNAsu gRhNIyAt kzatriyA Saram /
   vaiśyā pratodam ādadyād vedane tv agrajanmanaḥ // Yj_1.62 //	vESyA pratodam AdadyAt vedane tu agrajanmanaH // Yt-_1.62 //
   pitā pitāmaho bhrātā sakulyo jananī tathā /	pitA pitAmahaH BrAtA sakulyaH jananI taTA /

   grahādhīnā narendrāṇām ucchrāyāḥ patanāni ca /	graha-aDInAH narendrANAm ucCrAyAH patanAni ca /
   bhāvābhāvau ca jagatas tasmāt pūjyatamā grahāḥ // Yj_1.308 //	BAva-aBAvO ca jagataH tasmAt pUjyatamAH grahAH // Yt-_1.308 //
   grahāṇām idam ātithyaṃ kuryāt saṃvatsarād api /	grahANAm idam AtiTyam kuryAt saMvatsarAt api /
   ārogyabalasaṃpanno jīvet sa śaradaḥ śatam // Yj_1.308A //	Arogya-bala-saMpannaH jIvet sa SaradaH Satam // Yt-_1.308AH //
   [13. rājadharmaprakaraṇam]	[13. rAja-Darma-prakaraNam]
   mahotsāhaḥ sthūlalakṣaḥ kṛtajño vṛddhasevakaḥ /	mahA-utsAhaH sTUlalakzaH kRtajQaH vRdDa-sevakaH /
   vinītaḥ sattvasaṃpannaḥ kulīnaḥ satyavāk śuciḥ // Yj_1.309 //	vinItaH sattva-saMpannaH kulInaH satya-vAc SuciH // Yt-_1.309 //
   adīrghasūtraḥ smṛtimān akṣudro 'paruṣas tathā /	adIrGasUtraH smRtimAn akzudraH aparuzaH taTA /
   dhārmiko 'vyasanaś caiva prājñaḥ śūro rahasyavit // Yj_1.310 //	DArmikaH avyasanaH ca-eva prAjQaH SUraH rahasya-vid // Yt-_1.310 //
   svarandhragoptānvīkṣikyāṃ daṇḍanītyāṃ tathaiva ca /	sva-ranDra-goptA-AnvIkzikyAm daNxanItyAm taTA-eva ca /
   vinītas tv atha vārtāyāṃ trayyāṃ caiva narādhipaḥ // Yj_1.311 //	vinItaH tu aTa vArtAyAm trayyAm ca-eva narADipaH // Yt-_1.311 //
   sa mantriṇaḥ prakurvīta prājñān maulān sthirān śucīn /	sa mantriNaH prakurvIta prAjQAn mOlAn sTirAn SucIn /
   taiḥ sārdhaṃ cintayed rājyaṃ vipreṇātha tataḥ svayam // Yj_1.312 //	tEH sArDam cintayet rAjyam vipreNa-aTa tatas svayam // Yt-_1.312 //
   purohitaṃ prakurvīta daivajñam uditoditam /	purohitam prakurvIta dEva-jQam udita-uditam /
   daṇḍanītyāṃ ca kuśalam atharvāṅgirase tathā // Yj_1.313 //	daNxanItyAm ca kuSalam aTarva-aFgirase taTA // Yt-_1.313 //
   śrautasmārtakriyāhetor vṛṇuyād eva ca rtvijaḥ /	SrOta-smArta-kriyA-hetoH vRNuyAt eva ca rtvijaH /
   yajñāṃś caiva prakurvīta vidhivad bhūridakṣiṇān // Yj_1.314 //	yajQAn ca-eva prakurvIta viDivat BUri-dakziNAn // Yt-_1.314 //
   bhogāṃś ca dadyād viprebhyo vasūni vividhāni ca /	BogAn ca dadyAt vipreByaH vasUni viviDAni ca /

   askannam avyathaṃ caiva prāyaścittair adūṣitam /	askannam avyaTam ca-eva prAyaScittEH adUzitam /
   agneḥ sakāśād viprāgnau hutaṃ śreṣṭham ihocyate // Yj_1.316 //	agneH sakASAt vipra-agnO hutam SrezWam iha-ucyate // Yt-_1.316 //
   alabdham īhed dharmeṇa labdhaṃ yatnena pālayet /	alabDam Ihet DarmeNa labDam yatnena pAlayet /

   dattvā bhūmiṃ nibandhaṃ vā kṛtvā lekhyaṃ tu kārayet /	dattvA BUmim nibanDam vA kRtvA leKyam tu kArayet /
   āgāmibhadranṛpati- parijñānāya pārthivaḥ // Yj_1.318 //	AgAmiBadra-nRpati parijQAnAya pArTivaH // Yt-_1.318 //
   paṭe vā tāmrapaṭṭe vā svamudroparicihnitam /	pawe vA tAmra-pawwe vA sva-mudrA-upari-cihnitam /
   abhilekhyātmano vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ ca mahīpatiḥ // Yj_1.319 //	aBileKya-AtmanaH vaMSyAn AtmAnam ca mahIpatiH // Yt-_1.319 //
   pratigrahaparīmāṇaṃ dānacchedopavarṇanam /	pratigraha-parImANam dAna=-Ceda-upavarNanam /
   svahastakālasaṃpannaṃ śāsanaṃ kārayet sthiram // Yj_1.320 //	sva-hasta-kAla-saMpannam SAsanam kArayet sTiram // Yt-_1.320 //

   tatra tatra ca niṣṇātān adhyakṣān kuśalān śucīn /	tatra tatra ca nizNAtAn aDyakzAn kuSalAn SucIn /
   prakuryād āyakarmānta- vyayakarmasu codyatān // Yj_1.322 //	prakuryAt Aya-karmAnta vyaya-karmasu ca-udyatAn // Yt-_1.322 //
   nātaḥ parataro dharmo nṛpāṇāṃ yad raṇārjitam /	na-atas parataraH DarmaH nRpANAm yat raNa-arjitam /
   viprebhyo dīyate dravyaṃ prajābhyaś cābhayaṃ sadā // Yj_1.323 //	vipreByaH dIyate dravyam prajAByaH ca-aBayam sadA // Yt-_1.323 //
   ya āhaveṣu vadhyante bhūmyartham aparāṅmukhāḥ /	yaH Ahavezu vaDyante BUmi-arTam aparAFmuKAH /

   padāni kratutulyāni bhagneṣv avinivartinām /	padAni kratu-tulyAni Bagnezu avinivartinAm /

   na hanyād vinivṛttaṃ ca yuddhaprekṣaṇakādikam // Yj_1.326 //	na hanyAt vinivRttam ca yudDa-prekzaNaka-Adikam // Yt-_1.326 //

   hiraṇyaṃ vyāpṛtānītaṃ bhāṇḍāgāreṣu nikṣipet /	hiraNyam vyApRta-AnItam BANxAgArezu nikzipet /
   paśyec cārāṃs tato dūtān preṣayen mantrisaṃgataḥ // Yj_1.328 //	paSyet cArAn tatas dUtAn prezayet mantri-saMgataH // Yt-_1.328 //
   tataḥ svairavihārī syān mantribhir vā samāgataḥ /	tatas svEra-vihArI syAt mantriBiH vA samAgataH /
   balānāṃ darśanaṃ kṛtvā senānyā saha cintayet // Yj_1.329 //	balAnAm darSanam kRtvA senA-anyA saha cintayet // Yt-_1.329 //
   saṃdhyām upāsya śṛṇuyāc cārāṇāṃ gūḍhabhāṣitam /	saMDyAm upAsya SRNuyAt cArANAm gUXa-BAzitam /
   gītanṛtyaiś ca bhuñjīta paṭhet svādhyāyam eva ca // Yj_1.330 //	gIta-nRtyEH ca BuQjIta paWet svADyAyam eva ca // Yt-_1.330 //
   saṃviśet tūryaghoṣeṇa pratibudhyet tathaiva ca /	saMviSet tUrya-GozeNa pratibuDyet taTA-eva ca /
   śāstrāṇi cintayed buddhyā sarvakartavyatās tathā // Yj_1.331 //	SAstrANi cintayet budDyA sarva-kartavyatAH taTA // Yt-_1.331 //
   preṣayec ca tataś cārān sveṣv anyeṣu ca sādarān /	prezayet ca tatas cArAn svezu anyezu ca sAdarAn /
   ṛtvikpurohitācāryair āśīrbhir abhinanditaḥ // Yj_1.332 //	Rtvij-purohita-AcAryEH ASIrBiH aBinanditaH // Yt-_1.332 //
   dṛṣṭvā jyotirvido vaidyān dadyād gāṃ kāñcanaṃ mahīm /	dRzwvA jyotiH-vidaH vEdyAn dadyAt gAm kAQcanam mahIm /
   naiveśikāni ca tataḥ śrotriyebhyo gṛhāṇi ca // Yj_1.333 //	nEveSikAni ca tatas SrotriyeByaH gRhANi ca // Yt-_1.333 //
   brāhmaṇeṣu kṣamī snigdheṣv ajihmaḥ krodhano 'riṣu /	brAhmaNezu kzamI snigDezu ajihmaH kroDanaH arizu /
   syād rājā bhṛtyavargeṣu prajāsu ca yathā pitā // Yj_1.334 //	syAt rAjA BRtya-vargezu prajAsu ca yaTA pitA // Yt-_1.334 //
   puṇyāt ṣaḍbhāgam ādatte nyāyena paripālayan /	puNyAt zaz-BAgam Adatte nyAyena paripAlayan /
   sarvadānādhikaṃ yasmāt prajānāṃ paripālanam // Yj_1.335 //	sarva-dAna-aDikam yasmAt prajAnAm paripAlanam // Yt-_1.335 //
   cāṭataskaradurvṛtta- mahāsāhasikādibhiḥ /	cAwa-taskara-durvRtta mahA-sAhasikA-AdiBiH /
   pīḍyamānāḥ prajā rakṣet kāyasthaiś ca viśeṣataḥ // Yj_1.336 //	pIxyamAnAH prajAH rakzet kAyasTEH ca viSezataH // Yt-_1.336 //

   ye rāṣṭrādhikṛtās teṣāṃ cārair jñātvā viceṣṭitam /	ye rAzwra-aDikRtAH tezAm cArEH jQAtvA vicezwitam /
   sādhūn sammānayed rājā viparītāṃś ca ghātayet // Yj_1.338 //	sADUn sammAnayet rAjA viparItAn ca GAtayet // Yt-_1.338 //
   utkocajīvino dravya- hīnān kṛtvā vivāsayet /	utkoca-jIvinaH dravya hInAn kRtvA vivAsayet /
   saddānamānasatkārān śrotriyān vāsayet sadā // Yj_1.339 //	sat-dAna-mAna-satkArAn SrotriyAn vAsayet sadA // Yt-_1.339 //
   anyāyena nṛpo rāṣṭrāt svakośaṃ yo 'bhivardhayet /	anyAyena nRpaH rAzwrAt sva-koSam yaH aBivarDayet /
   so 'cirād vigataśrīko nāśam eti sabāndhavaḥ // Yj_1.340 //	saH acirAt vigata-SrIkaH nASam eti sa-bAnDavaH // Yt-_1.340 //
   prajāpīḍanasaṃtāpāt samudbhūto hutāśanaḥ /	prajA-pIxana-saMtApAt samudBUtaH hutASanaH /
   rājñaḥ kulaṃ śriyaṃ prāṇāṃś cādagdhvā na nivartate // Yj_1.341 //	rAjQaH kulam Sriyam prANAn ca-adagDvA na nivartate // Yt-_1.341 //
   ya eva nṛpater dharmaḥ svarāṣṭraparipālane /	yaH eva nRpateH DarmaH sva-rAzwra-paripAlane /
   tam eva kṛtsnam āpnoti pararāṣṭraṃ vaśaṃ nayan // Yj_1.342 //	tam eva kRtsnam Apnoti para-rAzwram vaSam nayan // Yt-_1.342 //
   yasmin deśe ya ācāro vyavahāraḥ kulasthitiḥ /	yasmin deSe yaH AcAraH vyavahAraH kula-sTitiH /
   tathaiva paripālyo 'sau yadā vaśam upāgataḥ // Yj_1.343 //	taTA-eva paripAlyaH asO yadA vaSam upAgataH // Yt-_1.343 //
   mantramūlaṃ yato rājyaṃ tasmān mantraṃ surakṣitam /	mantra-mUlam yatas rAjyam tasmAt mantram su-rakzitam /
   kuryād yathāsya na viduḥ karmaṇām āphalodayāt // Yj_1.344 //	kuryAt yaTA-asya na viduH karmaNAm APala-udayAt // Yt-_1.344 //
   arir mitram udāsīno 'nantaras tatparaḥ paraḥ /	ariH mitram udAsInaH anantaraH tad-paraH paraH /
   kramaśo maṇḍalaṃ cintyaṃ sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ // Yj_1.345 //	kramaSas maNxalam cintyam sAma-AdiBiH upakramEH // Yt-_1.345 //
   upāyāḥ sāma dānaṃ ca bhedo daṇḍas tathaiva ca /	upAyAH sAma dAnam ca BedaH daNxaH taTA-eva ca /
   samyakprayuktāḥ sidhyeyur daṇḍas tv agatikā gatiḥ // Yj_1.346 //	samyak-prayuktAH siDyeyuH daNxaH tu agatikA gatiH // Yt-_1.346 //
   saṃdhiṃ ca vigrahaṃ yānam āsanaṃ saṃśrayaṃ tathā /	saMDim ca vigraham yAnam Asanam saMSrayam taTA /
   dvaidhībhāvaṃ guṇān etān yathāvat parikalpayet // Yj_1.347 //	dvEDIBAvam guNAn etAn yaTAvat parikalpayet // Yt-_1.347 //
   yadā sasyaguṇopetaṃ pararāṣṭraṃ tadā vrajet /	yadA sasya-guNa-upetam para-rAzwram tadA vrajet /
   paraś ca hīna ātmā ca hṛṣṭavāhanapūruṣaḥ // Yj_1.348 //	paraH ca hInaH AtmA ca hRzwa-vAhana-pUruzaH // Yt-_1.348 //
   daive puruṣakāre ca karmasiddhir vyavasthitā /	dEve puruzakAre ca karma-sidDiH vyavasTitAH /
   tatra daivam abhivyaktaṃ pauruṣaṃ paurvadehikam // Yj_1.349 //	tatra dEvam aBivyaktam pOruzam pOrvadehikam // Yt-_1.349 //

   evaṃ puruṣakāreṇa vinā daivaṃ na sidhyati // Yj_1.351 //	evam puruzakAreNa vinA dEvam na siDyati // Yt-_1.351 //
   hiraṇyabhūmilābhebhyo mitralabdhir varā yataḥ /	hiraNya-BUmi-lABeByaH mitra-labDiH varAH yatas /
   ato yateta tatprāptyai rakṣet satyaṃ samāhitaḥ // Yj_1.352 //	atas yateta tad-prAptyE rakzet satyam samAhitaH // Yt-_1.352 //
   svāmy amātyā jano durgaṃ kośo daṇḍas tathaiva ca /	svAmI amAtyAH janaH durgam koSaH daNxaH taTA-eva ca /
   mitrāṇy etāḥ prakṛtayo rājyaṃ saptāṅgam ucyate // Yj_1.353 //	mitrANi etAH prakRtayaH rAjyam sapta-aFgam ucyate // Yt-_1.353 //

   dharmo hi daṇḍarūpeṇa brahmaṇā nirmitaḥ purā // Yj_1.354 //	DarmaH hi daNxa-rUpeNa brahmaNA nirmitaH purA // Yt-_1.354 //
   sa netuṃ nyāyato 'śakyo lubdhenākṛtabuddhinā /	sa netum nyAyataH aSakyaH lubDena-akRtabudDinA /
   satyasaṃdhena śucinā susahāyena dhīmatā // Yj_1.355 //	satya-saMDena SucinA su-sahAyena DImatA // Yt-_1.355 //

   samyak tu daṇḍanaṃ rājñaḥ svargakīrtijayāvaham // Yj_1.357 //	samyak tu daNxanam rAjQaH svarga-kIrti-jaya-Avaham // Yt-_1.357 //
   api bhrātā suto 'rghyo vā śvaśuro mātulo 'pi vā /	api BrAtA sutaH arGyaH vA SvaSuraH mAtulaH api vA /
   nādaṇḍyo nāma rājño 'sti dharmād vicalitaḥ svakāt // Yj_1.358 //	na-adaNxyaH nAma rAjQaH asti DarmAt vicalitaH svakAt // Yt-_1.358 //
   yo daṇḍyān daṇḍayed rājā samyag vadhyāṃś ca ghātayet /	yaH daNxyAn daNxayet rAjA samyak vaDyAn ca GAtayet /
   iṣṭaṃ syāt kratubhis tena samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ // Yj_1.359 //	izwam syAt kratuBiH tena samApta-vara-dakziNEH // Yt-_1.359 //
   iti saṃcintya nṛpatiḥ kratutulyaphalaṃ pṛthak /	iti saMcintya nRpatiH kratu-tulya-Palam pRTak /
   vyavahārān svayaṃ paśyet sabhyaiḥ parivṛto 'nvaham // Yj_1.360 //	vyavahArAn svayam paSyet saByEH parivRtaH anvaham // Yt-_1.360 //
   kulāni jātīḥ śreṇīś ca gaṇān jānapadān api /	kulAni jAtIH SreNIH ca gaNAn jAnapadAn api /

   jālasūryamarīcisthaṃ trasareṇū rajaḥ smṛtam /	jAla-sUrya-marIci-sTam trasareNuH rajaH smRtam /
   te 'ṣṭau likṣā tu tās tisro rājasarṣapa ucyate // Yj_1.362 //	te azwO likzA tu tAH tisraH rAjasarzapaH ucyate // Yt-_1.362 //
   gauras tu te trayaḥ ṣaṭ te yavo madhyas tu te trayaḥ /	gOraH tu te trayaH zaw te yavaH maDyaH tu te trayaH /
   kṛṣṇalaḥ pañca te māṣas te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa // Yj_1.363 //	kRzNalaH paQca te mAzaH te suvarNaH tu zoxaSa // Yt-_1.363 //
   palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ pañca vāpi prakīrtitam /	palam suvarNAH catvAraH paQca vA-api prakIrtitam /
   dve kṛṣṇale rūpyamāṣo dharaṇaṃ ṣoḍaśaiva te // Yj_1.364 //	dve kRzNale rUpya-mAzaH DaraNam zoxaSa-eva te // Yt-_1.364 //
   śatamānaṃ tu daśabhir dharaṇaiḥ palam eva tu /	SatamAnam tu daSaBiH DaraNEH palam eva tu /
   niṣkaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ kārṣikas tāmrikaḥ paṇaḥ // Yj_1.365 //	nizkam suvarNAH catvAraH kArzikaH tAmrikaH paNaH // Yt-_1.365 //
   sāśītipaṇasāhasro daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ /	sa-aSIti-paNa-sAhasraH daNxaH uttama-sAhasaH /
   tadardhaṃ madhyamaḥ proktas tadardham adhamaḥ smṛtaḥ // Yj_1.366 //	tad-arDam maDyamaH proktaH tad-arDam aDamaH smRtaH // Yt-_1.366 //
   dhigdaṇḍas tv atha vāgdaṇḍo dhanadaṇḍo vadhas tathā /	DigdaNxaH tu aTa vAgdaNxaH DanadaNxaH vaDaH taTA /
   yojyā vyastāḥ samastā vā hy aparādhavaśād ime // Yj_1.367 //	yojyAH vyastAH samastAH vA hi aparADa-vaSAt ime // Yt-_1.367 //
   jñātvāparādhaṃ deśaṃ ca kālaṃ balam athāpi vā /	jQAtvA-aparADam deSam ca kAlam balam aTa-api vA /
   vayaḥ karma ca vittaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet // Yj_1.368 //	vayaH karma ca vittam ca daNxam daNxyezu pAtayet // Yt-_1.368 //
   [End of the ācārādhyāya]	[Ent of Te AcAra-aDyAya]
   [II. vyavahārādhyāya]	[II. vyavahAra-aDyAya]
   [1. sādhāraṇavyavahāramātṛkāprakaraṇam]	[1. sADAraNa-vyavahAra-mAtRkA-prakaraNam]
   vyavahārān nṛpaḥ paśyed vidvadbhir brāhmaṇaiḥ saha /	vyavahArAn nRpaH paSyet vidvadBiH brAhmaNEH saha /
   dharmaśāstrānusāreṇa krodhalobhavivarjitaḥ // Yj_2.1 //	Darma-SAstra-anusAreNa kroDa-loBa-vivarjitaH // Yt-_2.1 //
   śrutādhyayanasaṃpannā dharmajñāḥ satyavādinaḥ /	Sruta-aDyayana-saMpannAH Darma-jQAH satya-vAdinaH /
   rājñā sabhāsadaḥ kāryā ripau mitre ca ye samāḥ // Yj_2.2 //	rAjQA saBAsadaH kAryAH ripO mitre ca ye samAH // Yt-_2.2 //
   apaśyatā kāryavaśād vyavahārān nṛpeṇa tu /	apaSyatA kArya-vaSAt vyavahArAn nRpeNa tu /
   sabhyaiḥ saha niyoktavyo brāhmaṇaḥ sarvadharmavit // Yj_2.3 //	saByEH saha niyoktavyaH brAhmaNaH sarva-Darma-vid // Yt-_2.3 //
   rāgāl lobhād bhayād vāpi smṛtyapetādikāriṇaḥ /	rAgAt loBAt BayAt vA-api smRti-apeta-Adi-kAriNaH /
   sabhyāḥ pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍyā vivādād dviguṇaṃ damam // Yj_2.4 //	saByAH pRTak pRTak daNxyAH vivAdAt dviguNam damam // Yt-_2.4 //
   smṛtyācāravyapetena mārgeṇādharṣitaḥ paraiḥ /	smRti-AcAra-vyapetena mArgeNa-ADarzitaH parEH /
   āvedayati ced rājñe vyavahārapadaṃ hi tat // Yj_2.5 //	Avedayati ced rAjQe vyavahAra-padam hi tat // Yt-_2.5 //
   pratyarthino 'grato lekhyaṃ yathāveditam arthinā /	pratyarTinaH agratas leKyam yaTA-veditam arTinA /
   samāmāsatadardhāhar- nāmajātyādicihnitam // Yj_2.6 //	samAmAsa-tad-arDAhar nAma-jAti-Adi-cihnitam // Yt-_2.6 //
   śrutārthasyottaraṃ lekhyaṃ pūrvāvedakasaṃnidhau /	Sruta-arTasya-uttaram leKyam pUrvAvedaka-saMniDO /
   tato 'rthī lekhayet sadyaḥ pratijñātārthasādhanam // Yj_2.7 //	tatas arTI leKayet sadyas pratijQAta-arTa-sADanam // Yt-_2.7 //
   tatsiddhau siddhim āpnoti viparītam ato 'nyathā /	tad-sidDO sidDim Apnoti viparItam atas anyaTA /
   catuṣpād vyavahāro 'yaṃ vivādeṣūpadarśitaḥ // Yj_2.8 //	catuzpAd vyavahAraH ayam vivAdezu-upadarSitaH // Yt-_2.8 //
   [2. asādhāraṇavyavahāramātṛkāprakaraṇam]	[2. asADAraNa-vyavahAra-mAtRkA-prakaraNam]
   abhiyogam anistīrya nainaṃ pratyabhiyojayet /	aBiyogam anistIrya na-enam pratyaBiyojayet /
   abhiyuktaṃ ca nānyena noktaṃ viprakṛtiṃ nayet // Yj_2.9 //	aBiyuktam ca na-anyena na-uktam viprakRtim nayet // Yt-_2.9 //
   kuryāt pratyabhiyogaṃ ca kalahe sāhaseṣu ca /	kuryAt pratyaBiyogam ca kalahe sAhasezu ca /
   ubhayoḥ pratibhūr grāhyaḥ samarthaḥ kāryanirṇaye // Yj_2.10 //	uBayoH pratiBUH grAhyaH samarTaH kArya-nirNaye // Yt-_2.10 //
   nihnave bhāvito dadyād dhanaṃ rājñe ca tatsamam /	nihnave BAvitaH dadyAt Danam rAjQe ca tad-samam /
   mithyābhiyogī dviguṇam abhiyogād dhanaṃ vahet // Yj_2.11 //	miTyA-aBiyogI dviguNam aBiyogAt Danam vahet // Yt-_2.11 //
   sāhasasteyapāruṣya- go'bhiśāpātyaye striyām /	sAhasa-steya-pAruzya go-aBiSApa-atyaye striyAm /

   deśād deśāntaraṃ yāti sṛkkiṇī parileḍhi ca /	deSAt deSa-antaram yAti sRkkiNI parileXi ca /
   lalāṭaṃ svidyate cāsya mukhaṃ vaivarṇyam eti ca // Yj_2.13 //	lalAwam svidyate ca-asya muKam vEvarNyam eti ca // Yt-_2.13 //
   pariśuṣyatskhaladvākyo viruddhaṃ bahu bhāṣite /	pariSuzyat-sKalat-vAkyaH virudDam bahu BAzite /
   vākcakṣuḥ pūjayati no tathauṣṭhau nirbhujaty api // Yj_2.14 //	vAc-cakzuH pUjayati no taTA-ozWO nirBujati api // Yt-_2.14 //

   na cāhūto vadet kiṃcid dhīno daṇḍyaś ca sa smṛtaḥ // Yj_2.16 //	na ca-AhUtaH vadet kiMcid DInaH daNxyaH ca sa smRtaH // Yt-_2.16 //

   dāpyaḥ sarvaṃ nṛpeṇārthaṃ na grāhyas tv aniveditaḥ // Yj_2.20 //	dApyaH sarvam nRpeNa-arTam na grAhyaH tu aniveditaH // Yt-_2.20 //

   pramāṇaṃ likhitaṃ bhuktiḥ sākṣiṇaś ceti kīrtitam /	pramANam liKitam BuktiH sAkziNaH ca-iti kIrtitam /

   paśyato 'bruvato bhūmer hānir viṃśativārṣikī /	paSyataH abruvataH BUmeH hAniH viMSati-vArzikI /
   pareṇa bhujyamānāyā dhanasya daśavārṣikī // Yj_2.24 //	pareNa BujyamAnAyAH Danasya daSa-vArzikI // Yt-_2.24 //

   [3. ṛṇādānaprakaraṇam]	[3. RNa-AdAna-prakaraNam]
   aśītibhāgo vṛddhiḥ syān māsi māsi sabandhake /	aSIti-BAgaH vRdDiH syAt mAsi mAsi sa-banDake /

   caritrabandhakakṛtaṃ sa vṛddhyā dāpayed dhanam /	caritra-banDaka-kRtam sa vRdDyA dApayet Danam /
   satyaṃkārakṛtaṃ dravyaṃ dviguṇaṃ pratidāpayet // Yj_2.61 //	satyaMkAra-kRtam dravyam dviguNam pratidApayet // Yt-_2.61 //

   tatkālakṛtamūlyo vā tatra tiṣṭhed avṛddhikaḥ /	tad-kAla-kRta-mUlyaH vA tatra tizWet avRdDikaH /
   vinā dhāraṇakād vāpi vikrīṇīta sasākṣikam // Yj_2.63 //	vinA DAraNakAt vA-api vikrINIta sa-sAkzikam // Yt-_2.63 //

   [4. upanidhiprakaraṇam]	[4. upaniDi-prakaraNam]

   [6. lekhyaprakaraṇam]	[6. leKya-prakaraNam]

   [8. dāyavibhāgaprakaraṇam]	[8. dAya-viBAga-prakaraNam]

   tanmantrasya ca bhettāraṃ chittvā jihvāṃ pravāsayet // Yj_2.302 //	tad-mantrasya ca BettAram CittvA jihvAm pravAsayet // Yt-_2.302 //

   rājayānāsanāroḍhur daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ // Yj_2.303 //	rAjayAna-Asana-AroXuH daNxaH uttama-sAhasaH // Yt-_2.303 //
   dvinetrabhedino rāja- dviṣṭādeśakṛtas tathā /	dvi-netra-BedinaH rAja dvizwa-AdeSa-kRtaH taTA /
   vipratvena ca śūdrasya jīvato 'ṣṭaśato damaḥ // Yj_2.304 //	vipra-tvena ca SUdrasya jIvataH azwaSataH damaH // Yt-_2.304 //
   durdṛṣṭāṃs tu punar dṛṣṭvā vyavahārān nṛpeṇa tu /	durdRzwAn tu punar dRzwvA vyavahArAn nRpeNa tu /
   sabhyāḥ sajayino daṇḍyā vivādād dviguṇaṃ damam // Yj_2.305 //	saByAH sa-jayinaH daNxyAH vivAdAt dviguNam damam // Yt-_2.305 //
   yo manyetājito 'smīti nyāyenāpi parājitaḥ /	yaH manyeta-ajitaH asmi-iti nyAyena-api parAjitaH /
   tam āyāntaṃ punar jitvā dāpayed dviguṇaṃ damam // Yj_2.306 //	tam AyAntam punar jitvA dApayet dviguNam damam // Yt-_2.306 //
   rājñānyāyena yo daṇḍo gṛhīto varuṇāya tam /	rAjQA-anyAyena yaH daNxaH gRhItaH varuNAya tam /
   nivedya dadyād viprebhyaḥ svayaṃ triṃśadguṇīkṛtam // Yj_2.307 //	nivedya dadyAt vipreByaH svayam triMSat-guNIkRtam // Yt-_2.307 //
   [End of the vyavahārādhyāya]	[Ent of Te vyavahAra-aDyAya]
   [III. prāyaścittādhyāyah]	[III. prAyaScitta-aDyAya-h]
   [1. āśaucaprakaraṇam]	[1. ASOca-prakaraNam]
   ūnadvivarṣaṃ nikhanen na kuryād udakaṃ tataḥ /	Una-dvi-varzam niKanet na kuryAt udakam tatas /
   āśmaśānād anuvrajya itaro jñātibhir vṛtaḥ // Yj_3.1 //	ASmaSAnAt anuvrajya itaraH jQAtiBiH vRtaH // Yt-_3.1 //
   yamasūktaṃ tathā gāthā japadbhir laukikāgninā /	yama-sUktam taTA gATAH japadBiH lOkika-agninA /
   sa dagdhavya upetaś ced āhitāgnyāvṛtārthavat // Yj_3.2 //	sa dagDavyaH upetaH ced AhitAgni-AvRta-arTa-vat // Yt-_3.2 //
   saptamād daśamād vāpi jñātayo 'bhyupayanty apaḥ /	saptamAt daSamAt vA-api jQAtayaH aByupayanti apaH /
   apa naḥ śośucad agham anena pitṛdiṅmukhāḥ // Yj_3.3 //	apa naH SoSucat aGam anena pitR-diFmuKAH // Yt-_3.3 //
   evaṃ mātāmahācārya- pretānām udakakriyā /	evam mAtAmaha-AcArya pretAnAm udaka-kriyA /

   sakṛt prasiñcanty udakaṃ nāmagotreṇa vāgyatāḥ /	sakRt prasiQcanti udakam nAma-gotreNa vAgyatAH /
   na brahmacāriṇaḥ kuryur udakaṃ patitās tathā // Yj_3.5 //	na brahmacAriNaH kuryuH udakam patitAH taTA // Yt-_3.5 //
   pākhaṇḍyanāśritāḥ stenā bhartṛghnyaḥ kāmagādikāḥ /	pAKaNxi-anASritAH stenAH BartR-GnyaH kAmagAdikAH /
   surāpya ātmatyāginyo nāśaucodakabhājanāḥ // Yj_3.6 //	surApyaH AtmatyAginyaH na-ASOca-udaka-BAjanAH // Yt-_3.6 //

   karmabhiḥ svaśarīrotthais tatra kā paridevanā // Yj_3.9 //	karmaBiH sva-SarIra-utTEH tatra kA paridevanAH // Yt-_3.9 //
   gantrī vasumatī nāśam udadhir daivatāni ca /	gantrI vasumatI nASam udaDiH dEvatAni ca /
   phenaprakhyaḥ kathaṃ nāśaṃ martyaloko na yāsyati // Yj_3.10 //	Pena-praKyaH kaTam nASam martya-lokaH na yAsyati // Yt-_3.10 //
   śleṣmāśru bāndhavair muktaṃ preto bhuṅkte yato 'vaśaḥ /	Slezma-aSru bAnDavEH muktam pretaH BuFkte yatas avaSaH /
   ato na roditavyaṃ hi kriyāḥ kāryāḥ svaśaktitaḥ // Yj_3.11 //	atas na roditavyam hi kriyAH kAryAH sva-SaktitaH // Yt-_3.11 //
   iti saṃśrutya gaccheyur gṛhaṃ bālapuraḥsarāḥ /	iti saMSrutya gacCeyuH gRham bAla-puraHsarAH /

   ahas tv adattakanyāsu bāleṣu ca viśodhanam /	ahar tu adatta-kanyAsu bAlezu ca viSoDanam /

   grāmād āhṛtya vā grāsān aṣṭau bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ /	grAmAt AhRtya vA grAsAn azwO BuQjIta vAgyataH /
   vāyubhakṣaḥ prāgudīcīṃ gacched vāvarṣmasaṃkṣayāt // Yj_3.55 //	vAyuBakzaH prAc-udIcIm gacCet vA-avarzma-saMkzayAt // Yt-_3.55 //
   [4. yatidharmaprakaraṇam]	[4. yati-Darma-prakaraNam]
